\subsection{Function Documentation}
\hypertarget{interp_8h_ad8633e9e18f6be8e8893df4add4bfbff}{\index{interp.\-h@{interp.\-h}!interp\-\_\-add\-Thread@{interp\-\_\-add\-Thread}}

\subsubsection[{interp\-\_\-add\-Thread}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf Pm\-Return\-\_\-t} interp\-\_\-add\-Thread (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf p\-Pm\-Func\-\_\-t}}]{pfunc}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{interp_8h_ad8633e9e18f6be8e8893df4add4bfbff}
Creates a thread object and adds it to the queue of threads to be executed while \hyperlink{interp_8c_ac70b009b0eca479fee502115ac4c911d}{interpret()} is running.

The given obj may be a function, module, or class. Creates a frame for the given function.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em pfunc} & Ptr to function to be executed as a thread. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Return status 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{interp_8h_ac51083e1fc01438996f83b94e08d50a8}{\index{interp.\-h@{interp.\-h}!interp\-\_\-reschedule@{interp\-\_\-reschedule}}
\index{interp\-\_\-reschedule@{interp\-\_\-reschedule}!interp.h@{interp.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{interp\-\_\-reschedule}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf Pm\-Return\-\_\-t} interp\-\_\-reschedule (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf void}}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{interp_8h_ac51083e1fc01438996f83b94e08d50a8}
Selects a thread to run and changes the V\-M internal variables to let the switch-\/loop execute the chosen one in the next iteration. For the moment the algorithm is primitive and will change the thread each time it is called in a round-\/robin fashion.
